className="section-page-name"><div class="js-branded-background-ads" id="wx-hero-content" className="js-branded-background-ads"></div><div class="hero hero-background layout-centered"><div class="hero-flex styles__heroFlex__3ulSz" className="hero-flex styles__heroFlex__3ulSz"></div></div><main class="content layout-centered"><region class="region region-main" aria-label="region-main" className="region region-main"><div id="main-Article-129074af-20f8-4e65-99f2-90fabba075cc"><div><div class="article-wrapper" className="article-wrapper"><div class="styles__articleContainer__7uJGn"><div class="style__collectionNameWrapper__1SU42" className="style__collectionNameWrapper__1SU42"><div class="style__collectionWrapper__WCWre"><h3 class="style__collectionName__1xjuo">MONSOON</h3><div class="wx-adWrapper  " style="" className="wx-adWrapper  "><div class="ad_module" id="WX_SpotLight" className="ad_module"></div></div></div><h1 class="style__articleTitle__3O08d">Maharashtra All Set to Commence Cloud Seeding in Drought-Hit Regions</h1><div class="style__header__2o89A"><h4>By <span class="style__authName__7aXu-"><a href="/en-IN/india/bios/">TWC India Edit Team</a></span></h4><h4>6 days ago</h4><h4>TWC India</h4></div></div><article class="styles__wrapper__aIsxE" aria-label="Maharashtra All Set to Commence Cloud Seeding in Drought-Hit Regions" className="styles__wrapper__aIsxE"><figure class="styles__imageWrapper__21RYZ" className="styles__imageWrapper__21RYZ"><div class="styles__image__1jgK5"><div class="styles__aspectRatioPlaceholder__2_6II" className="styles__aspectRatioPlaceholder__2_6II"><div style="padding-top:56.25%;"></div><div class="styles__progressiveMedia__ytAV_"><img class="image" src="https://s.w-x.co/util/image/w/in-plane_3.jpg?v=at&amp;w=485&amp;h=273" alt="" srcset="https://s.w-x.co/util/image/w/in-plane_3.jpg?v=at&amp;w=485&amp;h=273 400w, https://s.w-x.co/util/image/w/in-plane_3.jpg?v=ap&amp;w=980&amp;h=551 800w" className="image"><noscript>&amp;lt;img class=&quot;styles__noscript__2rw2y&quot; src=&quot;https://s.w-x.co/util/image/w/in-plane_3.jpg?v=at&amp;w=485&amp;h=273&quot; srcset=&quot;https://s.w-x.co/util/image/w/in-plane_3.jpg?v=at&amp;w=485&amp;h=273 400w, https://s.w-x.co/util/image/w/in-plane_3.jpg?v=ap&amp;w=980&amp;h=551 800w&quot; &amp;gt;</noscript></div></div><div class="styles__imgControls__1QEl8"><div class="styles__zoomContainer__2X4Fh" className="styles__zoomContainer__2X4Fh"><span class="styles__zoomIconSpan__1ryR9" className="styles__zoomIconSpan__1ryR9"><span class="icon icon-font iconset-ui styles__zoomIcon__vgN3U icon-zoom" className="icon icon-font iconset-ui styles__zoomIcon__vgN3U icon-zoom"></span></span></div></div></div><!--!--><figcaption><div class="styles__figcaption__3E2dj" className="styles__figcaption__3E2dj"><div class="styles__description__2zhsx" className="styles__description__2zhsx">Representational photo</div><span class="styles__credit__2Dkkv" className="styles__credit__2Dkkv">(Photo: K Sunil Prasad/ TOI, BCCL, BENGALURU
)</span></div></figcaption></figure><p>The Maharashtra government&#039;s Rs 31-crore cloud seeding project might kick off soon. Three planes that will be used to artificially induce rains in drought-hit Aurangabad, Solapur and Nagpur arrived at Solapur airport on July 23. The cloud-seeding exercise is expected to start in late July, and go on till the first week of August. </p><p>Last week, state agriculture minister Anil Bonde had told The Times of India that <a href="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/city/pune/maharashtra-govt-prepares-to-undertake-cloud-seeding/articleshow/70300142.cms">all permissions have been acquired</a><!----> to carry out the mission. He added that three Doppler radars had been set up, and that seeding can be done in a 400-kilometre radius of every radar. The news of the arrival of the planes is an indicator that the exercise, which is already long delayed, is set to commence very soon.</p><div><p>Maharashtra&#039;s water crisis has been steadily worsening since last year, particularly in drought-hit Vidarbha and Marathwada. Nearly two months into the monsoon--that officially begins on June 1--Marathwada and Vidarbha are facing rainfall deficits of 34% and 41% respectively (as on July 24) while Maharashtra is experiencing an overall 10% shortfall in rainfall. </p><div class="styles__paragraphAd__2La8d"><div class="LazyLoad" style="" className="LazyLoad"></div></div></div><p>As on July 23, dams in the state have just 25% water stock, compared to 46.5% stock during the same time last year. Shockingly, dams in Marathwada have just 0.82% of water.</p><p>The Maharashtra state government had conducted a similar cloud-seeding experiment over Marathwada in 2015 at a cost of Rs 27 crore, and that was labelled a success. Karnataka, too, has reportedly successfully implemented cloud-seeding last year. </p><p>An opposition party leader recently said that 1300 farmers in Maharashtra had committed suicide due to drought in the last six months. NCP spokesperson Nawab Malik wrote a Tweet accusing the state government of being apathetic to the plight of farmers.</p><!---->
</article></div><div class="style__disclaimer__3kgE8" className="style__disclaimer__3kgE8">The Weather Company’s primary journalistic mission is to report on breaking weather news, the environment and the importance of science to our lives. id=\"wxn0\" \u002F\u003E\u003Cp\u003EThe Maharashtra government's Rs 31-crore cloud seeding project might kick off soon. Three planes that will be used to artificially induce rains in drought-hit Aurangabad, Solapur and Nagpur arrived at Solapur airport on July 23. The cloud-seeding exercise is expected to start in late July, and go on till the first week of August. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003ELast week, state agriculture minister Anil Bonde had told The Times of India that \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Ftimesofindia.indiatimes.com\u002Fcity\u002Fpune\u002Fmaharashtra-govt-prepares-to-undertake-cloud-seeding\u002Farticleshow\u002F70300142.cms\"\u003Eall permissions have been acquired\u003C\u002Fa\u003E to carry out the mission. He added that three Doppler radars had been set up, and that seeding can be done in a 400-kilometre radius of every radar. The news of the arrival of the planes is an indicator that the exercise, which is already long delayed, is set to commence very soon.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EMaharashtra's water crisis has been steadily worsening since last year, particularly in drought-hit Vidarbha and Marathwada. Nearly two months into the monsoon--that officially begins on June 1--Marathwada and Vidarbha are facing rainfall deficits of 34% and 41% respectively (as on July 24) while Maharashtra is experiencing an overall 10% shortfall in rainfall. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EAs on July 23, dams in the state have just 25% water stock, compared to 46.5% stock during the same time last year. Shockingly, dams in Marathwada have just 0.82% of water.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EThe Maharashtra state government had conducted a similar cloud-seeding experiment over Marathwada in 2015 at a cost of Rs 27 crore, and that was labelled a success. Karnataka, too, has reportedly successfully implemented cloud-seeding last year. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EAn opposition party leader recently said that 1300 farmers in Maharashtra had committed suicide due to drought in the last six months. NCP spokesperson Nawab Malik wrote a Tweet accusing the state government of being apathetic to the plight of farmers.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n","flags":{"Facebook":true,"Intranet":false,"TV     <script>
      (function(p) {
        function getCookiesMap(t) {
          return t.split("; ").map(function(t) {
            return t.trim().split(/=(.+)/);
          }).reduce(function(t, i) {
            return t[i[0]] = i[1], t;
          }, {})
        }

        var cookieMap = getCookiesMap(document.cookie);
        var ciCookieMap = {};

        if (getCookiesMap(document.cookie).ci) {
          getCookiesMap(document.cookie).ci.split("&").forEach(function(t) {
            var parts = t.split('=');
            ciCookieMap[parts[0]] = parts[1];
          });
        }

        var regime = ciCookieMap && ciCookieMap['TWC-Privacy'] || 'exempt';

        var privacyPages = ['/en-US/twc/privacy-policy','/es-US/intl-privacy'];

        var isPrivacyPage = privacyPages.some(function(page) {
          return document.location.pathname.indexOf(page) > -1;
        });

        if (regime === 'exempt' && !isPrivacyPage) {
          var element = document.createElement('div');
          element.id = 'teconsent';
          element.className = 'truste-link';

          var truste_country ='IN';
          var truste_url = truste_country && 'https://consent.truste.com/notice?domain=weather.com&c=teconsent&country=IN' ||
                        'https://consent.truste.com/notice?domain=weather.com&c=teconsent';
          var sb = document.createElement('script');
          sb.src = truste_url;

          element.appendChild(sb)
          p.appendChild(element);
        } else {
          var element = document.createElement('div');
          element.id = "dpr-manager";
          p.appendChild(element);
        }
      })(
        document.getElementById('truste-container')
      )
    </script>
